Transmigrated Into An Evil Boss Destined To Die, He Survived By Tricking The System.

Channel: Zenitsu Recap Published: 2026-02-22 129,769 words Source: manual_caption

Transcript

Just like many other crazed players grinding levels to climb the server rankings, this young man also scrambled to join the Qian Continent. But as fate would have it, during one login attempt, the young man was electrocuted and transmigrated straight into the Qian Continent, becoming Sibin, an important character in this world. It was just a pity, that Sibin was an evil boss whose head everyone and their mother desperately wanted, because he was cruel, tyrannical, brutally despotic, massacred the common people, and was also debauched beyond measure, even humiliating Saintess Vu Y, whom everyone revered, causing her to eventually take her own life out of extreme humiliation. The protagonist himself, before transmigrating here, was the vanguard leading the army to fight the boss. After defeating Sibin, he even landed a sword strike on his manhood, as revenge for the girls he had harmed.

Yet, times changed too quickly; the dragon-slaying youth got electrocuted and became that very evil dragon. His life began once again, from when he was still crying in his father's arms. He seemed very proud to have this son and gave him the name Sibin of the Golden Lion family. After getting his new identity, Sibin was always haunted by the old plot. He swore that he would live a decent life, become a good lord, and love his people so that those players wouldn't come looking to settle scores.

After transmigrating, Sibin also activated a system. But this was the Strongest Villain System. Sibin vehemently refused; he didn't want to be a villain at all. But the system reminded him that he was a boss destined to die. Even though he had transmigrated into this body, Sibin couldn't change the main plot on his own.

In other words, he couldn't change the original owner's personality from a tyrannical lord into a good person. The only way to help Sibin escape his fated death was through the system's help, by continuously increasing his power, pushing the wheel of fate, and avoiding being hanged by the players. Sibin was speechless. He had transmigrated into a game, only to end up as someone destined to die. Could his life get any unluckier? If that was the case, his only option was to bind with the system.

After all, he still wanted to live. The system was quickly and successfully bound to Sibin. Afterward, he was informed that he needed to complete a series of villainous scenario quests, such as humiliating the saintess, slaughtering players, collecting subhuman female slaves, and so on. After completing the quests, he would receive rewards and the right to draw for functional rewards. Sibin thought about the scenario of humiliating the saintess, and then collecting those female slaves, and his cheeks flushed red.

It really wouldn't let him do anything remotely human, and even forced him down the path of a villain. He verbally expressed disdain, but just thinking about it made Sibin so excited he started drooling. However, wasn't it in the plot, that Lord Sibin was executed by the players after doing those immoral things? He didn't want to be like the original owner of this body. He also didn't want to kick the bucket. But the system reminded him that if he refused the quests, he wouldn't get any rewards.

At the same time, that damned system also presented Sibin with three future outcomes. First, being physically castrated by players. Second, being forced to turn into a loli. Third, death. The more Sibin listened, the worse his expression became; there wasn't a single bright path.

This damn system was clearly messing with him. Sibin felt his life was at a dead end. Struggling would lead to death, and doing nothing would also lead to death. He might as well live one day at a time and see if he could find a way to escape from this adversity. Outside, the butler was frantically knocking on Sibin's door.

Now that he mentioned it, today he had a horseback parade through the streets to present himself to the people as the new lord of this territory. Sibin dutifully performed his role, but he felt no joy in his heart. Sibin felt like he was now a monkey in a zoo. The people were constantly pointing, while he had absolutely no ability to resist his fate. Sibin wore that dejected face as he made a round through the square, then returned to his palace to officially present himself to the people.

At this point, it wasn't yet time for him to become the cruel tyrant reviled by thousands. So the people who came to see the new successor lord all chanted in unison the four words, "Long live the lord." After the long and tedious ceremony, Sibin was finally released back to his room. He was so tired it felt as if his limbs no longer belonged to him. But he hadn't rested for long before the series of villain quests was sent over. This meant Sibin wouldn't be at peace for much longer.

And the content of these quests was also very ridiculous. First was to snatch a lollipop from a child. Next was to trample a citizen's vegetable garden. Finally, to hang up an innocent commoner and beat them. Sibin felt these quests didn't resemble those of a tyrannical lord, but more like those of a hooligan.

But the system said that because these were newbie quests, they were this easy; it wouldn't be so easy later on, and he should understand and cherish it. After completing each quest, Sibin would get a chance to draw a prize. After completing all three quests, the probability of receiving a special reward would be unlocked. Although he still appeared indifferent on the surface, Sibin was actually craving those rewards. Well, since life was pushing him in this direction, he was forced to become a villainous bastard.

And so, without even taking a rest, he rushed out of his room. The dedicated butler was currently polishing a treasured sword. Sibin enthusiastically waved at him. "Come, let's go patrol the territory with your lord." Sibin rode a valiant red horse, eagerly galloping out of the castle, a very dangerous smile constantly on his face. Based on his many years of experience serving the young master, the butler immediately felt that something was not right.

Sibin's first target was a chubby kid. This child had also come to watch his coronation ceremony earlier. Both of them still remembered each other's faces. Sibin approached him with a business-like smile. "Since you know I'm the lord, doesn't that mean everyone has to listen to me, right?" The kid nodded, saying yes.

You couldn't blame him for being so easily swayed. Children are innocent; they say whatever they think. Immediately after, Sibin switched to a sweet, coaxing tone. "In that case, little friend, can you give me the candy in your hand?" This child was only a few years old and had no idea what the consequences of defying the lord would be. The candy in his hand was like his treasure.

Therefore, even if there were 10 lords here, he wouldn't agree. Sibin had expected this reaction. So he changed his tune, putting on a face like the boogeyman while growling out each word. "Give. It.

To. Me." The kid was terrified and immediately started wailing. The thing Sibin hated most was dealing with kids throwing a tantrum, with tears and snot everywhere like this, even though he was the one who made him cry in the first place. Sibin then promised the kid that if he gave him the candy, he would immediately give him two in return. Before the other party could even agree, a simulation screen appeared before Sibin.

"Bing! Host, don't think the system is a fool." Of course. So he couldn't bend the rules to both complete the quest and maintain his image as a kind and benevolent lord in the eyes of his people. However, the quest still needed to be completed. Therefore, Sibin resorted to forceful measures, decisively snatching the lollipop away. The kid fell to the ground, flailing about ceaselessly before the astonished eyes of the butler and the soldiers.

Sibin's mood wasn't great either. He felt that this quest of snatching candy from a child was even more humiliating than teasing the subhuman girls. The next quest was to trample the people's crops. Sibin chose the most fertile plot of land, where the crops were at their lushest. The owner of the field was even basking in the joy of an impending bumper harvest.

And yet, Sibin led a group of cavalrymen to dismount and they all competed to trample on it. The man who seemed to be the captain of this cavalry unit was utterly bewildered and turned to ask the butler, "What on earth is wrong with the Lord?" "Don't ask me, I don't know either." Only when the farmer's crops were completely destroyed did Sibin contentedly withdraw his men. Seeing the farmer's pained expression as his crops were destroyed, Sibin couldn't bear it either. He planned to secretly compensate him later after returning to claim his reward. The first two quests were complete, but the final one gave Sibin the biggest headache.

He didn't know how to handle it smoothly. How could he just hang up an innocent citizen for no reason and beat them? "Top-quality subhuman female slaves, reasonable prices here, first come, first served." While he was lost in thought, a voice struck Sibin's ears. As fate would have it, just when he was at a dead end, he came across a man hawking subhuman female slaves on the main street. It seemed a godsent opportunity had truly arrived. The moment he saw him, Sibin flashed a cunning smile, thinking to himself that it was lucky this unfortunate fellow had delivered himself to his doorstep.

And so, he was hung up and beaten, just as the script required. The reason given was that the new lord had issued a new decree: humans and the subhuman race must live together in peace, and from now on, Lam Dong City would not allow anyone to illegally trade subhumans. Thus, Sibin not only completed the quest but also moved those subhuman female slaves to tears. They all felt he was so compassionate and benevolent; having someone like him as their lord was a blessing for 18 generations of the subhuman race. Even the other citizens who gathered to watch felt that Sibin was wonderful, everyone who passed by had to stop and applaud.

After completing all three quests, Sibin hastily returned to the palace, and took off his cumbersome cloak. He demanded the system let him spin for his reward immediately. A spinning wheel appeared in front of Sibin. And this time, he received a set of perfect armor with the long, convoluted name "Shattered Dragon Heavy Armor Plate." Moreover, because he requested the reward only after completing all three quests, Sibin also received three extra chances for a reward critical hit. As a result, his perfect armor successfully got a critical hit and was upgraded to the "Hero Triumphant Saint Knight Hero Plate Mail." Although he didn't know what it did yet.

But Sibin only needed to hear the words "critical hit" and "hero" to know this was a rare treasure. He immediately equipped it, then wanted to find someone to test the capabilities of this new equipment. Sibin went to the training ground and ran into the butler, Crimon, who was practicing his swordsmanship there. He seemed surprised to see the young master, who was usually as lazy as a demon, voluntarily show up here today. Not only that, but Sibin also proactively suggested having a match with Crimon, reasoning that he had just acquired a decent set of armor.

It was then that the butler noticed his master's armor, which was shimmering with a golden light. This was the first time in his life Crimon had seen such a magnificent suit of armor. This armor of yours can't be described with just the words "not bad," it's truly too wonderful. Afterward, the two quickly stood on opposite sides of the training ground. Crimon would personally help the young master test the armor this new armor.

After greeting his opponent, he immediately rushed towards Sibin. Don't underestimate Crimon just because he's old. Although he was a butler, he was in fact also a great knight. Seeing Crimon's speed with his own eyes, Sibin also felt immense pressure. He took a step back to assume a defensive stance, then raised his sword.

The moment the two swords clashed, Sibin was a bit unsteady on his feet, but Crimon was knocked back. He had to use his feet as brakes, and it took quite a bit of effort for him to stop. It seemed Sibin's strength had improved a lot; he was no longer the useless young master Crimon once knew. On the opposite side, Sibin was extremely excited to see that his strength had indeed improved. The two continued to fight, with Crimon mostly on the attack, while he only dodged and evaded the blows.

But that was not simple at all, as his attacks were both fast and sharp. The two fought from the afternoon until evening. Both were exhausted, but Crimon still had to praise him profusely. The young master's new armor, combined with your own strength, its defensive effectiveness is truly first-rate. "It's because you went easy on me," Sibin replied modestly, but in reality, he was so pleased he was getting a big head.

He even carried that feeling of elation into his dreams that night. Sibin dreamed that he had unparalleled strength, single-handedly defeating an entire army of knights, and was even showered with praise by beautiful subhuman girls as well. In that dream, Sibin also dreamed that he was lying in a gaming pod for a virtual reality game and saw himself in the world of Qian Continent. This scene was far too terrifying, so he woke up with a start. Suddenly, that moment gave Sibin a bad premonition.

He felt as if he was being watched by someone. Just as his emotions were starting to settle, a simulation window suddenly appeared before him, scaring Sibin out of his wits. On it was a short notification: The players are preparing to come to Divine Light Town. "Wait, Divine Light Town? That name left a rather strong impression on Sibin. He suddenly recalled a war between the Goddess of the Wild, Malon, and the God of War and Flame, the Flame Dragon Bana.

Malon was a goddess with lower-tier power, while Bana was a god possessing mid-tier power. Therefore, this war was unbalanced from the very start. In the end, Malon was crushed in Bana's palm, and her divinity was shattered. Bana was also certain that the subhuman race she protected would eventually be annihilated. That was the first step that led to the subhuman race falling into slavery.

Sibin also remembered that a strange man had given the game's protagonist a blue crystal. He said that this item had the power to summon heroic spirits, and that the young man had to take it to save the subhuman people and end the endless oppression against them. These fragmented memories were all from the early stages of the game. It was just a pity that back then, Sibin never dreamed he would transmigrate into Qian Continent, so he had skipped quite a lot of the introductions. But based on those pieced-together recollections, Sibin could roughly guess that after the Goddess of the Wild's divinity shattered, she used her final strength to condense it into that mysterious crystal.

Afterward, that item was given to the game's protagonist by a mysterious character. This mysterious crystal was equivalent to the game's login client. And the heroic spirits the protagonist summoned through the crystal were the players. At first, when he was still a player, Sibin didn't feel there was anything wrong with this plot point. But now that he had transmigrated into the game and thought it over carefully, he felt that this world was fundamentally not just a game.

It was very real, and there was a high probability that these plot points were in fact the truth. And he was someone who had been summoned from Earth by a deity. That villain system was also sent along by the one who had summoned him. But as for that person's purpose, Sibin didn't know. He just felt that despite having no talent whatsoever, he could still become a pawn of a deity.

It sounded a bit self-deprecating, but this was truly the highest, supreme glory. Seeing Sibin muttering in the back, Crimon, who was driving the carriage in front, finally couldn't hold back his curiosity and asked: "Young Master Sibin, this old servant has a question. Why did you wake up so early today? And even take a carriage to Divine Light Town on the border of Eagle Crest Territory?" "Of course, it's to save my life," Sibin thought to himself. But he couldn't say these words out loud, so he started making things up. "I want to observe my territory a bit.

Mainly, I want to pay a surprise visit to the people. So let's start from Divine Light Town, the most remote border town." Seeing the young master being so mature, Crimon was so happy he couldn't stop smiling. He felt that after becoming a lord, Sibin was becoming more and more understanding and reasonable. In that case, the people in the territory would surely feel happy as well. But he also didn't forget to remind Sibin not to be too shocked after arriving at Divine Light Town.

Because the scenery here was extremely dilapidated. Until the flying carriage pulled by that giant eagle landed, Sibin still couldn't believe that what was in front of him was Divine Light Town. The name sounded grand, but the place was so dilapidated. "What kind of job did the previous lord do? Even if the land is barren and far from the royal capital, he shouldn't have turned a part of the territory into such a dump, right?" Sibin roared in anger. Seeing the young master so indignant, Crimon couldn't help but speak up to enlighten him a bit.

"The previous lord was Count Calante of the Iron Wall family. He was a fanatic of the god Flame Dragon Bana. So during his tenure, Calante was always off fighting battles and fighting battles, completely uninterested in managing his territory." In his memories, Sibin remembered Calante as a fat uncle who was always laughing heartily. He didn't expect that such a gentle-looking man would be of the warmongering type. "Um, actually, the previous area of our Eagle Crest Territory wasn't so large that we needed to use flying beasts to travel like we do now." Crimon said.

"Are you saying I should thank him for giving me an expanded version of Eagle Crest Territory?" Sibin retorted. But before Crimon could say another word, Sibin heard a commotion nearby. He followed the noisy sound and found a group of kids frantically beating up a little half-human, half-squirrel subhuman girl. As they beat her, they relentlessly cursed the little girl, calling her a lowly mongrel and telling her she should just hurry up and die. At that moment, Sibin wasn't the only one witnessing this unsightly scene.

Coincidentally, the protagonist of Qian Continent and a subhuman girl were also passing through the alley at that time. That girl was extremely anxious seeing one of her own kind being tormented like that. But the male protagonist didn't let her intervene, because he was afraid her identity would be exposed. He wanted to wait until the heroic spirits had condensed to save all the subhumans in Divine Light Town. "Do you want to save this one subhuman or all the subhumans in the town?" Although this guy wasn't wrong, the girl still couldn't bear the sight of her kin being tormented right before her eyes.

While she was still hesitating on how to resolve this situation, Sibin had already stepped forward before them. "What are you doing? Stop it!" His loud shout forced those vicious kids to stop. The male protagonist pulled the subhuman girl into a corner to observe. As for Sibin, he had absolutely no intention of forgiving these kids. Therefore, he immediately applied the rule of the right hand.

After spanking their butts until they were red as flowers, Sibin finally stopped. As he picked up the little subhuman girl and left, he unintentionally walked past the protagonist. The system immediately issued a warning that Sibin had discovered an important player nearby. The temporary system was also successfully upgraded and had many new functions. Sibin checked it out.

The most impressive new function was information data visualization. In other words, he could now see other people's information. It was just that the targets he could inspect were only those whose level was equal to or lower than his own. Sibin could also use it to check his own information. He currently held the status of a Count, and was also the lord of Eagle Crest Territory.

His strength was equivalent to a level 43 Earth Knight. Sibin also possessed a bunch of skills. His reputation in the Colon Empire was quite high, at 999 points. And after the incident of hanging that slave trader up to be beaten, he was also gradually gaining a reputation with the subhuman forces. Sibin was very satisfied to know he was a famous person.

But when he looked at Crimon, he suffered a serious blow. Because this old man not only had a higher level than him, but his reputation in the Colon Empire was as high as 13,721 points. Sibin felt as if he had suffered a blow that pierced his heart. Why did his bodyguard have a higher reputation than him? Putting that matter aside, Sibin continued to check the other functions. The second one was called Harvest Chains of Fate.

Specifically, each time Sibin escaped a fatal outcome, he would obtain one Chain of Fate. Although Sibin didn't know what this thing was specifically, it sounded strange. But the most important issue right now wasn't this thing called the Chains of Fate, but the mission at hand. He had to bring back the subhuman Saintess Zuy Y and humiliate her. Sibin felt cold sweat break out all over his head.

Saintess Rui was one of the biggest reasons the players rose up to hang Lord Sibin. When he was one of those players, he even volunteered to castrate him. Just thinking back on it now was enough to make him shiver. Perhaps understanding Sibin's confusion, the system later explained to him what the so-called Chains of Fate were. This item was used to seal the fate line of the child of fate, Ye Hao, who was the protagonist and the summoner of the other players.

Ye Hao's fate line has five branches, meaning Sibin must escape death five times and collect five Chains of Fate to completely seal and eliminate Ye Hao. But before that, he is not allowed to attack him under any subjective thought. As the child of fate, Ye Hao will receive the protection of the rules in this world. If Sibin hastily launches an attack, his identity might be exposed. Then, Ye Hao will directly target him, leading to the collapse of the world.

Apart from Ye Hao, Sibin can freely attack other players to ensure his own survival rate. Sibin was quite satisfied and found these rules reasonable. Aside from not being able to act against Ye Hao, he still had quite a lot of authority. And as the villain protagonist, how could he crush the righteous protagonist who was still in his budding stage? This was not in line with the rules at all. The first stage of the main storyline has been unlocked.

Now, Sibin can view it on the system at any time. And if Sibin remembered correctly, the masked girl with Ye Hao earlier was Saintess Rui. With his and the heroic spirits' help, the Saintess began to gradually take in and rescue the subhumans wandering everywhere on the border. But on one occasion, while the heroic spirits were rescuing a subhuman from a slave owner, they accidentally alerted the guards in Divine Light Town. They wanted to capture Saintess Rui and offer her to the lord.

That's why a conflict with Ye Hao occurred. It's just that these heroic spirits were also fierce and unafraid of death, so they just surrounded and attacked. In the end, victory belonged to Ye Hao's side. He and Rui seized control of Divine Light Town, establishing a firm foothold on the border of Eagle Crest Territory. Sibin, of course, would not let this happen as it did in his past life.

Ye Hao was directly causing trouble right before his eyes. Although he couldn't do anything to the protagonist, the system didn't say he couldn't touch the players either. It seemed many in this faction were about to get their asses kicked by Sibin. So, he and Crimon went to the mansion of the mayor of Divine Light Town. At first, Sibin was stopped by a man named Goodby.

He was the captain of this town's guard, an intermediate swordsman, level 13. In Divine Light Town, he was also considered a talented person, respected by the people. At first, Goodby was baring his fangs, but when he saw the golden lion emblem on Sibin's chest, he became cowardly. This emblem could only be worn by people of the empire or a lord. He hurriedly knelt.

This esteemed lord, I am the captain of the Divine Light Town guard, Goodby. May I ask what your orders are? Sibin silently assessed him, he was indeed a little impressed as this was a talented character in the game. He had two skills: Sweeping Cyclone and Valiant Assault. Moreover, these two skills could be used in a combination, with terrifying power. But according to the script in his past life, this captain was ultimately defeated by the players.

Only then was the boss of the Divine Light Town map, Mayor Mejin, revealed. To prevent that from happening, Sibin had to be one step ahead of the plot. He asked Goodby to call Mayor Mejin out to see him. Faced with that request, he seemed flustered. The mayor, he is busy, perhaps you could wait a moment, I will call him over.

Sibin didn't have time to wait. Ye Hao's appearance here proved that the players were also about to be summoned. So he walked directly into the mansion. What Goodby called 'busy' was actually Mejin being busy fooling around, with a scantily clad, long-legged beauty in each arm. Seeing Sibin kick the door open and barge in, he didn't know his place and yelled loudly.

Who is it, don't you want to live anymore? Can't you see that this mayor is busy? But as soon as he saw the other person's face, Mejin was so scared his soul nearly left his body. He hurriedly pushed away the two scantily clad beauties in his arms and knelt before Sibin. Esteemed Young Master Sibin, oh no, Esteemed Lord. This old servant prayed day and night to the god of luck, and you have finally graced us with your presence. Why didn't you give a heads-up so this old servant could personally welcome you? Sibin himself was utterly disdainful of the old man's so-called 'busyness'.

If he had given notice, he wouldn't have seen this scene. However, Sibin couldn't be bothered to care about that matter. Because what concerned him more now was Mejin's mediocre ability, not at all worthy of being the boss of this map. The guy only had the strength of a level 11 knight, with two skills: Mount and Charge, and Mounted Spear Assault. However, these two skills could only be used on horseback, otherwise, Mejin was truly useless.

Moreover, he was the type of person hated by both humans and subhumans. Yet, upon seeing Sibin, Mejin still had the gall to boast that Divine Light Town had been very peaceful recently. Sibin scoffed. Mejin's sycophantic attitude had already made him very displeased. Now, the word 'peaceful' coming from the guy's mouth was even more grating to his ears.

Sibin pointed at the man's face, breathing fire. Peaceful my ass, subhumans have already infiltrated your room, and you don't know a damn thing. If that's the case, don't sit in this mayor's seat anymore. I'll be the mayor, you be the captain of the guard here for me. When you've understood things clearly, only then will I reinstate you.

A moment later, Goodby saw Sibin storming out of the mansion. Mejin was crying behind him, repeatedly saying he couldn't do it. But no matter how much he cried, he couldn't make Sibin change his mind. Sibin forced Mejin to immediately stand guard here and properly perform the duties of the guard captain. Even the old man's horse was confiscated by Sibin.

After hearing this, Goodby's soul flew to the clouds. Now, it wasn't just Mejin hugging his leg and crying, but Goodby joined in the fun as well. "My lord, this really won't do. If he becomes the guard captain, what will I do?" Annoyed by the two men hugging his left and right legs, Sibin yelled. "You'll be my personal guard, double the allowance." Upon hearing the words 'double the allowance,' Goodby immediately stopped crying, flashed a bright smile, and agreed.

It's true that material possessions determine consciousness. After giving his orders, Sibin rode out on his horse, taking the injured subhuman girl with him. Before leaving, he didn't forget to order Goodby to prepare a clean room and a large, comfortable bed for him. Mejin watched Sibin's departing back, an unwilling expression clear on his face. He even thought he was being pressured like this because he hadn't presented a gift in time when Sibin took office.

So this brat likes subhumans, and he still pretends to be noble and righteous with me, Mejin thought to himself. Afterwards, he ordered his subordinates to find some beautiful subhuman slaves and bring them to the mayor's mansion, with the ambition of soon reclaiming the mayor's seat for himself. After taking the subhuman girl to be treated, Sibin brought her back to the mayor's residence. He carried the girl straight into the room that Goodby had prepared. The child was still unconscious.

Seeing the two twitching squirrel ears and tail, Sibin almost couldn't resist reaching out to stroke them. Just then, the child woke up. Sibin thought to himself, "Oh no," this time I'll be misunderstood for harassing her. But unexpectedly, the first thing the little girl said was: "I'm sorry, my lord, I didn't mean to dirty your bedsheets. I don't know how I ended up here either, I'm sorry." Seeing the girl's pitiful, trembling appearance, Sibin was about to speak to comfort her.

But right after, the child was so scared she knelt and begged him not to take her life. Sibin was extremely flustered. Was his appearance really that scary, to frighten a child to this extent? I rescued you, why would I take your life? Try to remember carefully. At that time, you were being bullied by a group of brats until you fainted. It was I who beat them to a pulp and brought you here.

At this, the little girl calmed down a bit. "Lory remembers now. But Lory didn't faint from being hit, I fainted from hunger." As soon as she finished speaking, her stomach rumbled loudly, making her blush with embarrassment. In this situation, Sibin couldn't be so inhumane as to continue starving the girl named Lory. So he ordered his subordinates to prepare a table full of food.

Lory was so hungry her vision blurred, she greedily stuffed bread into her mouth while constantly thanking him. Seeing the child eat with such an appetite, Sibin also felt happy. But right after, that damn system appeared again and brought a not-so-happy notification. It turned out that this overly humane act was not at all in line with the usual behavior of a villain. The system demanded that Sibin stop immediately, or he would be punished.

But after a few times, Sibin had realized that this system wasn't too rigid and its rules could be bent. Therefore, he retorted that he had saved this subhuman child to raise her as his pawn. At a critical moment, the girl would become the one to backstab the players and the protagonist, Ye Hao. The system was spun around by him like a top, to the point of being speechless. After analyzing Sibin's behavior for a while, it determined that the plan he just mentioned was feasible.

Therefore, it quickly updated his villainous behavior protocol. In the future, Sibin would no longer be warned for similar situations. Sibin was extremely pleased, silently cursing that shabby system for being so stupid. Luckily, he had already understood its fatal weakness; as long as he rationalized the motive for his actions, he wouldn't be punished. After that, the system began to update the daily villain missions.

Today, like the day before, there were three missions. First, Sibin had to leave a psychological scar on 10 or more players. Next, he had to force Lory to give him a shoulder massage and warm his bed. Finally, Sibin had to humiliate the protagonist, Ye Hao, to receive a reward. Looking at these missions, Sibin was so shocked he slammed the table and stood up.

Lory was currently stuffing a chicken leg into her mouth. The little girl thought Sibin was angry because she was eating too much, so she timidly offered the chicken leg to him, though she was still quite reluctant. "Esteemed Lord, you eat." I'm not asking for your food, kid. Also, don't call me Esteemed Lord anymore. I am the Count of Eagle Crest Territory, my name is Sibin of the Golden Lion Clan.

Speaking of which, Sibin suddenly had a wicked idea. Lory had just said she wanted to repay him. Then this was the most suitable time, as Sibin happened to be in need of a maid. So he invited the girl to take that position, with the promise of three full meals a day and two days off a week. Meanwhile, at the largest subhuman slave farm in town, the farm owner was frantically beating the pitiful subhuman girls.

Just then, a few guards on horseback arrived, saying that the mayor wanted some beautiful slaves. Seeing this, the farm owner obsequiously tried to curry favor, saying that he had just captured a few slaves, all of them glistening and smooth, who would surely please the mayor. With that said, he turned back, intending to whip the poor girls again. But this time, before the whip could even fall, it was stopped by a strong arm. it turned out the players had already appeared in Divine Light Town.

A person named Lin Fan led a few other players and bravely charged straight into the slave trading camp. "Stop, don't you know that human trafficking is against the law?" "Subhumans are people?" "You brat, are you here to cause trouble?" The farm owner struggled free and retorted. Lin Fan was momentarily speechless; he had forgotten that this world was fake, and its legal system was nothing like the real world's, so he decided to handle it differently. Lin Fan tossed a bag of money into the farm owner's hands, then declared he would buy all of these slaves. Inside were brand-new gold coins.

Seeing this, the farm owner's expression changed completely. "Esteemed guest, these slaves have already been reserved by Lord Mayor Sibin. If you want subhuman slaves, please wait a moment." Lin Fan was half-believing, half-doubting, because before coming here, he had heard the dungeon boss was Mejin. Why had it changed to Sibin now? Could this be a game bug? However, while Lin Fan was still confused, the players following him could no longer hold back. They all drew their swords and threatened the farm owner to release the subhuman slaves immediately.

The moment the farm owner saw the blades, he was scared out of his wits and hastily fled. And right at this moment, Mejin appeared. Although he had been stripped of his mayoral status by Sibin, he was still the boss of this dungeon. And even though Sibin looked down on this guy for being as weak as a snail, to new level-two and level-three players like Lin Fan, the level-11 Mejin still posed a huge threat. Not to mention the skills and equipment of the two sides were also too different.

In that situation, they could only hope for Ye Hao's help. And this guy, true to his role as a righteous protagonist, always appeared just in time. As soon as Ye Hao arrived, he quickly activated the skill Sacred Shield Fortress. With his support, the other players immediately became much more confident, charging straight towards Mejin together. Everyone wanted to take down the boss to get equipment.

Thus, the old man's health bar dropped rapidly, and in the end, he was defeated by a Radiant Cross Slash from Ye Hao. The group of players stared at each other blankly. Ye Hao was the main character of the story, but in the end, he was still just an NPC. What kind of game design was this, where an NPC ended up kill-stealing the boss from the players? Lin Fan also found it hard to understand. They had fought so hard, and the boss only had a sliver of health left.

In the end, the main character rushed in to kill-steal the last hit, and he even looked so magnificent doing it. After defeating Mejin, Ye Hao looked very relaxed. He then turned back to the group of players to announce something. It was that they had helped a lot in taking down this boss. Therefore, the weapons, armor, and all the wealth Mejin had accumulated belonged to them.

Only then did Lin Fan's group stop grumbling. It was fine to let the main character shine. As long as they still got rewards in the end, it was all good. So, the whole group trooped over to the mansion of Mejin. But as soon as they arrived, they came across Sibin standing imposingly, waiting for them.

The moment he saw the players arrive, Sibin put on a tough act, using his coldest voice to intimidate them. "You harmed my guards, killed my servant, and now you want to steal my money. To cause such a ruckus in my territory, you're really quite arrogant, aren't you?" The players looked at each other blankly; they didn't know who Sibin was or why he was here. Because at this early stage of the game, Sibin shouldn't be able to appear in this place. Lin Fan immediately used an appraisal skill to check the opponent.

The result was that apart from the name Sibin Golden Lion, level 44, and his identity as the Lord of Eagle Crest Territory, they saw nothing else. Just a level-11 Mejin required Ye Hao's help for them to defeat. Now a level-44 Sibin had shown up, who could possibly beat him? More importantly, why was the Lord of Eagle Crest Territory here? Shouldn't you be sitting comfortably in your lord's castle ? The group of players began to curse out the game developers. Making players in the newbie village face a final boss, level-two players fighting a level-44 boss. This was truly making a game with their knees.

However, even though Sibin was a nightmare-level boss, these players still harbored the ambition of taking him down. Because just think about it, how much good equipment and rewards would drop after defeating him. Of course, they didn't have the ability to do that.
